name:Aâ€nâ€oâ€nâ€yâ€mâ€oâ€uâ€sâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r

rating:4.2
posted:Posted April 15, 2024
msg:This hotel is a little far from the city. We drove here from Taiping Ancient City. It is obvious that this is a new district. Next to the hotel is Mixc, opposite is a school, and behind is a building, but it is still under renovation. The whole environment is relatively quiet. The hotel is on the 9th floor, with a good view, overlooking the mountains and rivers, and Mixc and the gymnasium on the other side. The sound insulation effect is also OK, and it is more stable to sleep at night.
Disadvantages:
1. The lifting screen is relatively new, but the projection machine has some problems, and it is seriously stuck. At the beginning, it said that there was no signal when I clicked on the live TV. For movies and TV, I chose a movie in the free zone and it was stuck, and then it was directly "frozen". The projection screen said that it was not in the same network as the mobile phone. In short, I couldn't watch it. I couldn't call the front desk phone from the room. Finally, I could only use my own mobile phone to call, and then I contacted and asked the staff to fix it.
2. The welcome fruit didn't feel fresh, suspected that it was a bit moldy, and I didn't dare to eat it.
3. After using the hair dryer for a while, I don't know whether it was due to charging or cooling, but it can't be used when it is turned on again. It needs to be used for a while.
4. The socket of the bedside table near the window can't be used and can't be charged.
I hope the hotel can conduct corresponding investigations and rectifications.
Finally, I would like to thank the hotel, because sometimes I carelessly left my bracelet in the room and found it in the afternoon. I asked the hotel to find it twice and finally found it and help to send it back. Thank you very much. I hope the hotel can get better and better after improvement.

msg:The hotel opened in 2023. The facade is average, and the lobby is not impressive. There are ground and underground parking lots for convenient parking. The room is super large, with good sound insulation, a 65-inch TV, and accurate air conditioning control. There is no desk in the room, only a round table in the middle, which is not convenient to plug in. The bed and quilt are OK, but the pillow is too high. There is a "switch button instructions" sign in the room, which needs to be studied carefully. I don't know how to control the light switch. It's too fancy and not practical. There are few varieties of breakfast and the quality is average. Only the freshly cooked noodles and rice noodles are good, with minced meat and barbecued pork.
The hotel is located in a relatively remote location, but there is a MixC shopping mall next to it, with some restaurants to choose from.
